### Tizin VOS Translation for ‚ÄúI like apples‚Äù Using Maktay and Zapple

**TASK**: In the fictional language of Tizin, basic sentences are arranged with the Verb first, followed by the direct object, followed by the subject of the sentence. I want to express my love for apples to my Tizin friend.

The word that indicates oneself is "Pa" is the nominative form, "Mato" is the accusative form, and "Sing" is the genitive form.

The root verb that indicates an intense like for something is "Maktay". When it is used in the present, it is used in it's root form, when it is used in the preterit past, it is "Tay", and when it is used in the imperfect past, it is "Aktay". It is used differently than in English, and is better translated as "is pleasing to", meaning that the thing doing the liking is actually the object of the sentence rather than the subject.

The word for apples is borrowed from English in Tizin, and so it is "Apple" is the nominative form, "Zapple" is the accusative form, and "Izapple" is the genitive form.

Please translate "I like apples" to Tizin.

```
{
"role": 'planner',
"plan": '<END>',
"description": "Task completed successfully through direct linguistic analysis. Based on the Tizin grammar rules provided: (1) Sentence structure is Verb-Object-Subject, (2) 'Maktay' means 'is pleasing to' in present tense, (3) The thing being liked (apples) becomes the subject in nominative form 'Apple', (4) The person doing the liking (I) becomes the object in accusative form 'Mato'. Therefore, 'I like apples' translates to 'Maktay Mato Apple' in Tizin. Final answer: Maktay Mato Apple",
}
```

```
print(f'\nSearch {i}: {query[:50]}...')

page=1,
backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"],
safesearch="off",

)

print(f'Found {len(results)} results')

# Extract data directly without complex scoping

# Create combined text for analysis - simple and direct

print(f' Result {j}: {len(text)} chars')

# Direct analysis without complex variables
evidence_found = []
relevance = 0

evidence_found.append('WWII damage reference')
relevance += 8

if 'burnley' in text:
evidence_found.append('Burnley connection')
relevance += 8
print(' üè≠ Burnley connection!')

if 'victorian' in text:
evidence_found.append('Victorian era reference')
relevance += 6
print(' üèõÔ∏è Victorian era reference!')

# Store findings if relevant
if relevance >= 8 or len(evidence_found) >= 2:
finding = {
'search_number': i,
'result_number': j,
'query': query,
'title': title,
'body': body[:300], # Truncate for storage
'url': url,
'relevance_score': relevance,
'evidence': evidence_found
}

all_findings.append(finding)
all_evidence.extend(evidence_found)

print(f' üìã STORED: Score {relevance}, Evidence: {", ".join(evidence_found)}')
print(f' Title: {title[:80]}...')
else:
print('No results found')

except Exception as e:
```

### Development Step 6: Surrey Lodge South London: Victorian Origins, Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Damage, Burnley Move

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Museum exhibition curation: Conduct automated web searches and timeline analysis to verify Surrey Lodge‚Äôs architectural changes, temperance hall conversion, and WWII damage for accurate exhibit signage and narrative content.
- Heritage consultancy for planning permissions: Compile historical evidence of Victorian-era developments, rotating stage installations, and bomb damage to support restoration and planning applications for listed building consent.
- Academic publication on the Victorian temperance movement: Systematically extract founding organization details, key dates, and transformation events at Surrey Lodge for inclusion in a peer-reviewed history journal article.
- Cultural preservation grant writing: Assemble a detailed chronology of Surrey Lodge‚Äôs conversion into a temperance hall, first rotating stage installation, and wartime repairs to strengthen grant proposals for heritage conservation funding.
- Legal property due diligence: Trace documented structural modifications, WWII bomb damage references, and subsequent company relocation records to resolve title disputes and inform conveyancing reports.
- Urban historical mapping project: Automate targeted searches and relevance scoring to integrate Surrey Lodge‚Äôs development timeline and relocation data into a digital heritage GIS for local authority archives.
- Industrial heritage documentary production: Gather precise dates and primary‚Äêsource snippets about the UK‚Äôs first rotating stage in 1935 and Surrey Lodge‚Äôs wartime story to script an educational documentary segment.
- Genealogical estate research: Use comprehensive search queries and timeline extraction to uncover ancestral connections to Surrey Lodge, detailing original ownership, temperance hall use, and post-Blitz relocation for family history publications.

```
from ddgs import DDGS
import os
import json
import time
from collections import Counter

try:
# Execute search

max_results=10,
page=1,
backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"],
safesearch="off",
region="en-us"
)

if results:
print(f'Found {len(results)} results')

# Initialize query findings

'query': query,
'search_number': i,

}

'surrey lodge': 10,

}

# CRITICAL FIX: Define full_text in same scope where it's used

for term, weight in key_terms.items():

relevance_score += weight

historical_indicators.append('Surrey Lodge confirmed')
print(' üéØ Surrey Lodge confirmed!')

historical_indicators.append('1935 rotating stage date confirmed')

else:

research_results['search_queries'].append(query)

except Exception as e:

}

# Calculate research success rate
```

### Development Step 2: Surrey Lodge History: Victorian Beginnings, Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Bombing, Burnley Relocation

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Municipal heritage teams automating extraction of Victorian-era building histories from archived city council websites for preservation grant applications
- Academic history researchers compiling precise timelines of 19th-century social movement venues by analyzing saved HTML search results from digital archives
- Theatre technology historians identifying early rotating stage installations by scanning periodicals and hall websites for 1930s date references
- Insurance risk assessors evaluating wartime bomb damage liabilities by mining online council bomb-damage records and compiled archive pages
- Corporate due diligence analysts tracking legacy company relocations by parsing historical press releases and relocation notices from archived web pages
- Digital librarians structuring metadata on temperance movement meeting halls by extracting organizational founding details from library web archives
- Real estate developers reviewing heritage constraints by retrieving structural transformation records and wartime impact data from municipal HTML archives
- Cultural tourism planners building interactive timelines of historical London landmarks by consolidating extracted event dates and site transformations from saved HTML

```
import os
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re
from collections import Counter

print('=== SURREY LODGE HISTORICAL ANALYSIS - FIXING SEARCH RESULTS PROCESSING ===')

'surrey lodge': 10,

'temperance': 8,
'temperance hall': 10,
'victorian': 6,
'rotating stage': 10,
'1935': 8,
'first rotating stage': 12,

# Read HTML content
with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

print(f'File size: {len(html_content):,} characters')

# Parse HTML content - FIXED: Proper variable scope
soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Extract text content - FIXED: Ensure page_text is properly defined
page_text = soup.get_text().lower()
print(f'Extracted text: {len(page_text):,} characters')

# Calculate relevance score
found_terms = []
relevance_score = 0

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in page_text:
found_terms.append(term)
relevance_score += weight

print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}')
print(f'Found terms ({len(found_terms)}): {', '.join(found_terms[:8])}')

# Extract specific historical indicators
historical_indicators = []

# Look for Surrey Lodge mentions
if 'surrey lodge' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Surrey Lodge confirmed')
print('üéØ SURREY LODGE CONFIRMED!')

# Look for temperance hall references
if 'temperance hall' in page_text or ('temperance' in page_text and 'hall' in page_text):
historical_indicators.append('Temperance hall connection found')
print('üèõÔ∏è TEMPERANCE HALL CONNECTION FOUND!')

# Look for rotating stage references
if 'rotating stage' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Rotating stage reference found')
print('üé≠ ROTATING STAGE REFERENCE FOUND!')

if '1935' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('1935 rotating stage date confirmed')
print('üìÖ 1935 DATE CONFIRMED!')

# Look for WWII/bomb damage
if any(term in page_text for term in ['bomb damage', 'bombed', 'war damage', 'blitz']):
historical_indicators.append('WWII damage reference found')
print('üí• WWII DAMAGE REFERENCE FOUND!')

# Look for Burnley connection
if 'burnley' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Burnley connection found')
print('üè≠ BURNLEY CONNECTION FOUND!')

# Extract relevant text snippets for context
text_snippets = []
sentences = page_text.split('.')

for sentence in sentences:
sentence = sentence.strip()
if len(sentence) > 20 and len(sentence) < 400:
# Look for sentences containing key terms
if 'surrey lodge' in sentence:
text_snippets.append(sentence)
elif any(term in sentence for term in ['temperance hall', 'rotating stage', 'burnley', '1935']):
text_snippets.append(sentence)

# Remove duplicates and limit
unique_snippets = list(set(text_snippets))[:5]

if unique_snippets:
print(f'Key text snippets found ({len(unique_snippets)}):')
for j, snippet in enumerate(unique_snippets[:3], 1):
print(f' {j}. {snippet[:200]}...')

# Look for dates and timeline information
timeline_info = []
date_patterns = ['1935', '193[0-9]', '19[0-4][0-9]', 'victorian', 'world war', 'wwii']

for sentence in sentences:
sentence = sentence.strip()
if len(sentence) > 15 and len(sentence) < 300:
# Check if sentence contains date-related information
if any(pattern.replace('[0-9]', '') in sentence for pattern in date_patterns):
timeline_info.append(sentence)

# Remove duplicates from timeline info
unique_timeline = list(set(timeline_info))[:3]

# Store analysis results
file_analysis = {

'found_terms': found_terms,
'historical_indicators': historical_indicators,
'text_snippets': unique_snippets,
'timeline_information': unique_timeline
}

analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis)
analysis_results['historical_findings'].extend(historical_indicators)
analysis_results['timeline_information'].extend(unique_timeline)

# Show high-relevance findings
if relevance_score >= 15 or len(historical_indicators) >= 2:
print(f'üìö HIGH RELEVANCE FINDING - Score: {relevance_score}, Indicators: {len(historical_indicators)}')
elif relevance_score > 0:
print(f'üìù Moderate relevance - Score: {relevance_score}')
else:
print('‚ùå Low relevance - no key terms found')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error processing {html_file}: {str(e)}')
# Continue with next file instead of stopping
continue

print('\n=== PHASE 3: COMPREHENSIVE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS ===')
print('=' * 80)

total_files = len(analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'])
print(f'Successfully analyzed files: {total_files}')

if total_files > 0:
# Sort files by relevance score
analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)

print('\nüìä RELEVANCE RANKING:')
print('-' * 40)

high_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 15]
moderate_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if 5 <= f['relevance_score'] < 15]
low_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if f['relevance_score'] < 5]

print(f'High relevance files (15+ points): {len(high_relevance)}')
print(f'Moderate relevance files (5-14 points): {len(moderate_relevance)}')
print(f'Low relevance files (0-4 points): {len(low_relevance)}')

if high_relevance:
print('\nüéØ TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FILES:')
for i, file_data in enumerate(high_relevance[:3], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. {file_data["filename"]}:')
print(f' Score: {file_data["relevance_score"]}')
print(f' Terms: {', '.join(file_data["found_terms"][:6])}')
print(f' Indicators: {', '.join(file_data["historical_indicators"])}')
if file_data.get('text_snippets'):
print(f' Sample text: {file_data["text_snippets"][0][:150]}...')

# Analyze all historical indicators
all_indicators = analysis_results['historical_findings']
indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators)

print('\nüìà HISTORICAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:')
print('-' * 45)
for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common():
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} files')

# Evidence analysis for each focus area
evidence_analysis = {
'surrey_lodge_identified': 'Surrey Lodge confirmed' in all_indicators,
'temperance_hall_connection': 'Temperance hall connection found' in all_indicators,
'rotating_stage_1935': 'Rotating stage reference found' in all_indicators and '1935 rotating stage date confirmed' in all_indicators,
'wwii_damage_confirmed': 'WWII damage reference found' in all_indicators,
'burnley_relocation': 'Burnley connection found' in all_indicators
}

print('\nüîç FOCUS AREA EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 45)
for area, confirmed in evidence_analysis.items():
status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå'
print(f'{status} {area.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}')

analysis_results['evidence_summary'] = evidence_analysis

# Calculate research success rate
```

### Development Step 3: Surrey Lodge: Origins, Victorian Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Damage, Burnley Relocation

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Heritage architecture research for conservation specialists analyzing Surrey Lodge‚Äôs Victorian origins, temperance hall transformation, and WWII damage to inform restoration projects
- Digital archiving for local history museums automating extraction of founding organization details, rotating stage installation in 1935, and relocation events to create enriched exhibit metadata
- Curriculum development for history educators generating interactive timelines and textual snippers about Surrey Lodge‚Äôs evolution for classroom modules on South London heritage
- Urban planning risk assessment for property developers evaluating past bomb damage, historical uses, and relocation patterns of sites like Surrey Lodge to guide redevelopment proposals
- Genealogy support tools for family historians mining HTML archives for references to temperance organizations and community halls where ancestors may have participated
- Cultural tourism itinerary building for guide operators compiling thematic tours that highlight Surrey Lodge‚Äôs first rotating stage and other unique historical milestones
- Academic digital humanities research on tracing organizational transformations and societal impact by scraping web records for evidence of Victorian temperance movements and subsequent relocations
- Heritage insurance underwriting systems assessing structural history, wartime damages, and refurbishment records of listed buildings such as Surrey Lodge to calculate coverage and premiums

from ddgs import DDGS import os import json import time from collections import Counter print('=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE SEARCH - CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION ===') print('Objective: Identify historic area with 19th-century bathhouse, traditional houses, blue-tiled minaret') print('Focus: Shebeke windows with 5000+ pieces, mirrored balconies, wall paintings, 8-year construction') print('APPROACH: Clean implementation with proper variable handling and error prevention\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize research results with clean structure research_data = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features', 'target_features': [ '19th-century bathhouse still in use', 'Traditional Azerbaijani houses with verandas and stained-glass windows', 'Building with blue-tiled minaret', 'Shebeke windows with over 5,000 handcrafted pieces', 'Mirrored balconies', 'Historical wall paintings', 'Eight years for decorative embellishment' ], 'searches_completed': [], 'all_findings': [], 'location_evidence': {}, 'architectural_features': {}, 'construction_timeline': [] } print('TARGET ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for i, feature in enumerate(research_data['target_features'], 1): print(f' {i}. {feature}') # Define focused search queries search_queries = [ 'Azerbaijan historic area 19th century bathhouse traditional houses', 'Sheki Azerbaijan Shebeke windows 5000 pieces handcrafted', 'Azerbaijan blue-tiled minaret traditional architecture district', 'Azerbaijan Khan Palace mirrored balconies wall paintings', 'Azerbaijan traditional houses verandas stained glass windows', 'Azerbaijan historic bathhouse hammam 19th century still operating', 'Sheki Azerbaijan historic architecture Shebeke windows construction', 'Azerbaijan Shebeke windows eight years construction decorative embellishment' ] print(f'\nExecuting {len(search_queries)} focused searches:') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) print('\n=== PHASE 1: CLEAN SEARCH EXECUTION ===') print('=' * 70) # Execute searches with clean error handling for search_num, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {search_num}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Execute search search_results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if search_results: print(f'Found {len(search_results)} results') # Process each result with clean variable handling search_findings = [] for result_num, result in enumerate(search_results, 1): try: # CLEAN APPROACH: Define all variables at start with safe defaults result_title = result.get('title', '') result_body = result.get('body', '') result_url = result.get('href', '') # Create combined text for analysis - PROPERLY SCOPED combined_text = f"{result_title} {result_body}".lower() print(f' Result {result_num}: {len(combined_text)} chars') # Define architectural indicators indicators_found = [] relevance_score = 0 # Check for Azerbaijan if 'azerbaijan' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Azerbaijan confirmed') relevance_score += 8 print(' üá¶üáø Azerbaijan confirmed!') # Check for Sheki location if 'sheki' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Sheki location identified') relevance_score += 12 print(' üèõÔ∏è Sheki location identified!') # Check for blue minaret if 'blue minaret' in combined_text or 'blue-tiled minaret' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Blue-tiled minaret found') relevance_score += 12 print(' üïå Blue-tiled minaret found!') # Check for Shebeke windows if 'shebeke' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Shebeke windows reference found') relevance_score += 15 print(' ü™ü Shebeke windows found!') if '5000' in combined_text or '5,000' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed') relevance_score += 12 print(' üé® 5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed!') # Check for mirrored balconies if 'mirrored balconies' in combined_text or 'mirror balcon' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Mirrored balconies found') relevance_score += 12 print(' ü™û Mirrored balconies found!') # Check for wall paintings if 'wall paintings' in combined_text or 'wall painting' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Wall paintings reference found') relevance_score += 10 print(' üé® Wall paintings found!') # Check for construction time if 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Eight years construction time found') relevance_score += 10 print(' ‚è∞ Eight years construction time found!') # Check for traditional houses with verandas if 'traditional houses' in combined_text and ('verandas' in combined_text or 'veranda' in combined_text): indicators_found.append('Traditional houses with verandas found') relevance_score += 10 print(' üè† Traditional houses with verandas found!') # Check for stained glass if 'stained glass' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Stained glass windows found') relevance_score += 8 print(' üåà Stained glass windows found!') # Store relevant findings if relevance_score >= 8 or len(indicators_found) > 0: finding = { 'search_number': search_num, 'result_number': result_num, 'query': query, 'title': result_title, 'body': result_body[:300], # Store search completion research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': len(search_results), 'findings_count': len(search_findings) }) else: print('‚ùå No results found') research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': 0, 'findings_count': 0 }) except Exception as search_error: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(search_error)}') research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'error': str(search_error) }) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: COMPREHENSIVE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS') print('=' * 80) total_searches = len(research_data['searches_completed']) successful_searches = len([s for s in research_data['searches_completed'] if 'error' not in s]) total_findings = len(research_data['all_findings']) print(f'Search execution summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {total_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') if research_data['all_findings']: # Compile all indicators all_indicators = [] for finding in research_data['all_findings']: all_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) # Analyze evidence frequency indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators) print('\nüìà ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 50) for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions') # Calculate success rate confirmed_count = sum(feature_analysis.values()) success_rate = (confirmed_count / len(feature_analysis)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_rate:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(feature_analysis)} features confirmed)') research_data['success_rate'] = success_rate # Sort findings by relevance research_data['all_findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:') print('-' * 50) for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['all_findings'][:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score: {finding["relevance_score"]} | Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])}') print(f' Title: {finding["title"][:100]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Content: {finding["body"][:120]}...') # Analyze location evidence location_mentions = {} for finding in research_data['all_findings']: combined_content = f"{finding['title']} {finding['body']}".lower() # Check for location mentions locations = ['sheki', 'ganja', 'baku', 'gabala', 'quba', 'lahij', 'shamakhi'] for location in locations: if location in combined_content: location_mentions[location] = location_mentions.get(location, 0) + 1 if location_mentions: research_data['location_evidence'] = location_mentions print('\nüó∫Ô∏è LOCATION EVIDENCE:') print('-' * 30) sorted_locations = sorted(location_mentions.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) for location, count in sorted_locations: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {location.title()}: {count} mentions') # from ddgs import DDGS import os import json import time from collections import Counter print('=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE SEARCH - CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION ===') print('Objective: Identify historic area with 19th-century bathhouse, traditional houses, blue-tiled minaret') print('Focus: Shebeke windows with 5000+ pieces, mirrored balconies, wall paintings, 8-year construction') print('APPROACH: Clean implementation with proper variable handling and error prevention\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize research results with clean structure research_data = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features', 'target_features': [ '19th-century bathhouse still in use', 'Traditional Azerbaijani houses with verandas and stained-glass windows', 'Building with blue-tiled minaret', 'Shebeke windows with over 5,000 handcrafted pieces', 'Mirrored balconies', 'Historical wall paintings', 'Eight years for decorative embellishment' ], 'searches_completed': [], 'all_findings': [], 'location_evidence': {}, 'architectural_features': {}, 'construction_timeline': [] } print('TARGET ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for i, feature in enumerate(research_data['target_features'], 1): print(f' {i}. {feature}') # Define focused search queries search_queries = [ 'Azerbaijan historic area 19th century bathhouse traditional houses', 'Sheki Azerbaijan Shebeke windows 5000 pieces handcrafted', 'Azerbaijan blue-tiled minaret traditional architecture district', 'Azerbaijan Khan Palace mirrored balconies wall paintings', 'Azerbaijan traditional houses verandas stained glass windows', 'Azerbaijan historic bathhouse hammam 19th century still operating', 'Sheki Azerbaijan historic architecture Shebeke windows construction', 'Azerbaijan Shebeke windows eight years construction decorative embellishment' ] print(f'\nExecuting {len(search_queries)} focused searches:') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) print('\n=== PHASE 1: CLEAN SEARCH EXECUTION ===') print('=' * 70) # Execute searches with clean error handling for search_num, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {search_num}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Execute search search_results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if search_results: print(f'Found {len(search_results)} results') # Process each result with clean variable handling search_findings = [] for result_num, result in enumerate(search_results, 1): try: # CLEAN APPROACH: Define all variables at start with safe defaults result_title = result.get('title', '') result_body = result.get('body', '') result_url = result.get('href', '') # Create combined text for analysis - PROPERLY SCOPED combined_text = f"{result_title} {result_body}".lower() print(f' Result {result_num}: {len(combined_text)} chars') # Define architectural indicators indicators_found = [] relevance_score = 0 # Check for Azerbaijan if 'azerbaijan' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Azerbaijan confirmed') relevance_score += 8 print(' üá¶üáø Azerbaijan confirmed!') # Check for Sheki location if 'sheki' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Sheki location identified') relevance_score += 12 print(' üèõÔ∏è Sheki location identified!') # Check for bathhouse if 'bathhouse' in combined_text or 'hammam' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Bathhouse reference found') relevance_score += 10 print(' üõÅ Bathhouse reference found!') if '19th century' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('19th century bathhouse confirmed') relevance_score += 8 print(' üìÖ 19th century bathhouse confirmed!') # Check for blue minaret if 'blue minaret' in combined_text or 'blue-tiled minaret' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Blue-tiled minaret found') relevance_score += 12 print(' üïå Blue-tiled minaret found!') # Check for Shebeke windows if 'shebeke' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Shebeke windows reference found') relevance_score += 15 print(' ü™ü Shebeke windows found!') if '5000' in combined_text or '5,000' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed') relevance_score += 12 print(' üé® 5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed!') # Check for mirrored balconies if 'mirrored balconies' in combined_text or 'mirror balcon' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Mirrored balconies found') relevance_score += 12 print(' ü™û Mirrored balconies found!') # Check for wall paintings if 'wall paintings' in combined_text or 'wall painting' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Wall paintings reference found') relevance_score += 10 print(' üé® Wall paintings found!') # Check for construction time if 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Eight years construction time found') relevance_score += 10 print(' ‚è∞ Eight years construction time found!') # Check for traditional houses with verandas if 'traditional houses' in combined_text and ('verandas' in combined_text or 'veranda' in combined_text): indicators_found.append('Traditional houses with verandas found') relevance_score += 10 print(' üè† Traditional houses with verandas found!') # Check for stained glass if 'stained glass' in combined_text: indicators_found.append('Stained glass windows found') relevance_score += 8 print(' üåà Stained glass windows found!') # Store relevant findings if relevance_score >= 8 or len(indicators_found) > 0: finding = { 'search_number': search_num, 'result_number': result_num, 'query': query, 'title': result_title, 'body': result_body[:300], # Truncate for storage 'url': result_url, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'indicators': indicators_found } search_findings.append(finding) research_data['all_findings'].append(finding) print(f' üìã STORED: Score {relevance_score}, Indicators: {", ".join(indicators_found)}') print(f' Title: {result_title[:80]}...') # Add to construction timeline if relevant if any(term in combined_text for term in ['years', 'century', 'built', 'constructed']): timeline_entry = f"{result_title} - {result_body[:150]}" research_data['construction_timeline'].append(timeline_entry) except Exception as result_error: print(f' ‚ùå Error processing result {result_num}: {str(result_error)}') continue # Show search summary print(f'\nüìä Search Summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant findings: {len(search_findings)}/{len(search_results)}') if search_findings: all_indicators = [] for finding in search_findings: all_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators) top_indicators = [f"{ind}({count})" for ind, count in indicator_counts.most_common(3)] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top indicators: {", ".join(top_indicators)}') # Store search completion research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': len(search_results), 'findings_count': len(search_findings) }) else: print('‚ùå No results found') research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': 0, 'findings_count': 0 }) except Exception as search_error: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(search_error)}') research_data['searches_completed'].append({ 'query': query, 'error': str(search_error) }) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: COMPREHENSIVE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS') print('=' * 80) total_searches = len(research_data['searches_completed']) successful_searches = len([s for s in research_data['searches_completed'] if 'error' not in s]) total_findings = len(research_data['all_findings']) print(f'Search execution summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {total_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') if research_data['all_findings']: # Compile all indicators all_indicators = [] for finding in research_data['all_findings']: all_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) # Analyze evidence frequency indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators) print('\nüìà ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 50) for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions') # Analyze architectural features feature_analysis = { 'azerbaijan_confirmed': 'Azerbaijan confirmed' in all_indicators, 'sheki_location': 'Sheki location identified' in all_indicators, 'bathhouse_19th_century': ('Bathhouse reference found' in all_indicators and '19th century bathhouse confirmed' in all_indicators), 'blue_tiled_minaret': 'Blue-tiled minaret found' in all_indicators, 'shebeke_5000_pieces': ('Shebeke windows reference found' in all_indicators and '5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed' in all_indicators), 'mirrored_balconies': 'Mirrored balconies found' in all_indicators, 'wall_paintings': 'Wall paintings reference found' in all_indicators, 'eight_years_construction': 'Eight years construction time found' in all_indicators, 'traditional_houses_verandas': 'Traditional houses with verandas found' in all_indicators, 'stained_glass_windows': 'Stained glass windows found' in all_indicators } research_data['architectural_features'] = feature_analysis print('\nüîç ARCHITECTURAL FEATURE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 50) for feature, confirmed in feature_analysis.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå' print(f'{status} {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}') # Calculate success rate confirmed_count = sum(feature_analysis.values()) success_rate = (confirmed_count / len(feature_analysis)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_rate:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(feature_analysis)} features confirmed)') research_data['success_rate'] = success_rate # Sort findings by relevance research_data['all_findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:') print('-' * 50) for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['all_findings'][:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score: {finding["relevance_score"]} | Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])}') print(f' Title: {finding["title"][:100]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Content: {finding["body"][:120]}...') # Analyze location evidence location_mentions = {} for finding in research_data['all_findings']: combined_content = f"{finding['title']} {finding['body']}".lower() # Check for location mentions locations = ['sheki', 'ganja', 'baku', 'gabala', 'quba', 'lahij', 'shamakhi'] for location in locations: if location in combined_content: location_mentions[location] = location_mentions.get(location, 0) + 1 if location_mentions: research_data['location_evidence'] = location_mentions print('\nüó∫Ô∏è LOCATION EVIDENCE:') print('-' * 30) sorted_locations = sorted(location_mentions.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) for location, count in sorted_locations: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {location.title()}: {count} mentions') # Identify primary location candidate if sorted_locations: primary_location = sorted_locations[0] research_data['primary_location'] = primary_location[0] print(f'\nüéØ PRIMARY LOCATION CANDIDATE: {primary_location[0].title()} ({primary_location[1]} mentions)') else: print('‚ùå No findings collected') # Save research results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_architecture_research_clean.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ RESEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Create summary report summary_content = f'''AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE RESEARCH CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION RESULTS Generated: {research_data["timestamp"]} RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features: ''' for feature in research_data['target_features']: summary_content += f'‚Ä¢ {feature}\n' summary_content += f''' SEARCH EXECUTION: ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {len(research_data["searches_completed"])} ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len([s for s in research_data["searches_completed"] if "error" not in s])} ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {len(research_data["all_findings"])} ''' if research_data.get('success_rate'): summary_content += f'‚Ä¢ Research success rate: {research_data["success_rate"]:.1f}%\n' if research_data.get('primary_location'): summary_content += f'‚Ä¢ Primary location candidate: {research_data["primary_location"].title()}\n' summary_content += f''' ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES ANALYSIS: ''' if research_data.get('architectural_features'): for feature, confirmed in research_data['architectural_features'].items(): status = 'CONFIRMED' if confirmed else 'NOT FOUND' summary_content += f'‚Ä¢ {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {status}\n' summary_content += f''' TOP FINDINGS: ''' for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['all_findings'][:3], 1): summary_content += f'''{i}. {finding["title"]} URL: {finding["url"]} Relevance Score: {finding["relevance_score"]} Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])} Content: {finding["body"][:150]}... ''' summary_content += '''FILES GENERATED: ‚Ä¢ azerbaijan_architecture_research_clean.json - Complete research data ‚Ä¢ azerbaijan_architecture_clean_summary.txt - This summary report ''' # Save summary report summary_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_architecture_clean_summary.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(summary_content) print(f'üìã SUMMARY REPORT SAVED TO: {summary_file}') print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE RESEARCH COMPLETE - CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION') print('=' * 90) if research_data.get('success_rate', 0) >= 60: print('‚úÖ RESEARCH HIGHLY SUCCESSFUL - Multiple architectural features identified') elif research_data.get('success_rate', 0) >= 40: print('‚ö†Ô∏è RESEARCH MODERATELY SUCCESSFUL - Several features found') else: print('‚ùå LIMITED SUCCESS - Further targeted research recommended') print('\nüìä FINAL RESEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search queries executed: {len(research_data["searches_completed"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len([s for s in research_data["searches_completed"] if "error" not in s])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {len(research_data["all_findings"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Unique indicators: {len(set(all_indicators)) if research_data["all_findings"] else 0}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Timeline references: {len(research_data["construction_timeline"])}') if research_data.get('primary_location'): print(f'\nüéØ PRIMARY LOCATION: {research_data["primary_location"].title()}') if research_data.get('architectural_features'): confirmed_features = [feature.replace('_', ' ').title() for feature, confirmed in research_data['architectural_features'].items() if confirmed] if confirmed_features: print('\nüèõÔ∏è CONFIRMED ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for feature in confirmed_features: print(f' ‚úÖ {feature}') print('\n=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE CLEAN RESEARCH COMPLETE ===')

from ddgs import DDGS import os import json import time from collections import Counter print('=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE SEARCH - FINAL FIXED IMPLEMENTATION ===') print('Objective: Identify historic area with 19th-century bathhouse, traditional houses, blue-tiled minaret') print('Focus: Shebeke windows with 5000+ pieces, mirrored balconies, wall paintings, 8-year construction') print('CRITICAL FIX: Consistent variable naming - using combined_text throughout\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize research results with clean structure research_data = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features', 'target_features': [ '19th-century bathhouse still in use', 'Traditional Azerbaijani houses with verandas and stained-glass windows', 'Building with blue-tiled minaret', 'Shebeke windows with over 5,000 handcrafted pieces', 'Mirrored balconies', 'Historical wall paintings', 'Eight years for decorative embellishment' ], 'searches_completed': [], 'all_findings': [], 'location_evidence': {}, 'architectural_features': {}, 'construction_timeline': [] } print('TARGET ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for i, feature in enumerate(research_data['target_features'], 1): print(f' {i}. {feature}') # Define focused search queries search_queries = [ 'Azerbaijan historic area 19th century bathhouse traditional houses', 'Sheki Azerbaijan Shebeke windows 5000 pieces handcrafted', 'Azerbaijan blue-tiled minaret traditional architecture district', 'Azerbaijan Khan Palace mirrored balconies wall paintings', 'Azerbaijan traditional houses verandas stained glass windows', 'Azerbaijan historic bathhouse hammam 19th century still operating', 'Sheki Azerbaijan historic architecture Shebeke windows construction', 'Azerbaijan Shebeke windows eight years construction decorative embellishment' ] print(f'\nExecuting {len(search_queries)} focused searches:') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) print('\n=== PHASE 1: FIXED SEARCH EXECUTION ===') print('=' * 70) # Execute searches with consistent variable naming for search_num, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {search_num}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Execute search search_results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if search_results: print(f'Found {len(search_results)} results') # Process each result with consistent variable naming search_findings = [] for result_num, result in enumerate(search_results, 1): try: # FIXED: Define all variables at start with consistent naming result_title = result.get('title', '') result_body = result.get('body', '') result_url = result.get('href', '') # from ddgs import DDGS import os import json import time from collections import Counter print('=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE SEARCH - SIMPLIFIED CLEAN APPROACH ===') print('Objective: Identify historic area with 19th-century bathhouse, traditional houses, blue-tiled minaret') print('Focus: Shebeke windows with 5000+ pieces, mirrored balconies, wall paintings, 8-year construction') print('APPROACH: Simplified implementation with bulletproof variable handling\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize clean research structure research_data = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features', 'target_features': [ '19th-century bathhouse still in use', 'Traditional Azerbaijani houses with verandas and stained-glass windows', 'Building with blue-tiled minaret', 'Shebeke windows with over 5,000 handcrafted pieces', 'Mirrored balconies', 'Historical wall paintings', 'Eight years for decorative embellishment' ], 'search_results': [], 'findings': [], 'evidence': {}, 'locations': {} } print('TARGET ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for i, feature in enumerate(research_data['target_features'], 1): print(f' {i}. {feature}') # Define focused search queries queries = [ 'Azerbaijan historic area 19th century bathhouse traditional houses', 'Sheki Azerbaijan Shebeke windows 5000 pieces handcrafted', 'Azerbaijan blue-tiled minaret traditional architecture district', 'Azerbaijan Khan Palace mirrored balconies wall paintings', 'Azerbaijan traditional houses verandas stained glass windows', 'Azerbaijan historic bathhouse hammam 19th century still operating' ] print(f'\nExecuting {len(queries)} searches:') for i, query in enumerate(queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Initialize searcher searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) print('\n=== PHASE 1: CLEAN SEARCH EXECUTION ===') print('=' * 60) # Execute searches with simple, clean processing for search_idx, query in enumerate(queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {search_idx}/{len(queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 50) try: results = searcher.text( query, max_results=8, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') search_findings = [] for result_idx, result in enumerate(results, 1): # BULLETPROOF: Define all variables at the very start title_text = str(result.get('title', '')) body_text = str(result.get('body', '')) url_text = str(result.get('href', '')) # BULLETPROOF: Create analysis text with safe concatenation analysis_text = (title_text + ' ' + body_text).lower() print(f' Result {result_idx}: {len(analysis_text)} chars') # Simple indicator detection found_indicators = [] score = 0 # Check each indicator separately with bulletproof logic if 'azerbaijan' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Azerbaijan confirmed') score += 8 print(' üá¶üáø Azerbaijan confirmed!') if 'sheki' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Sheki location identified') score += 12 print(' üèõÔ∏è Sheki location identified!') if 'bathhouse' in analysis_text or 'hammam' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Bathhouse reference found') score += 10 print(' üõÅ Bathhouse reference found!') if '19th century' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('19th century bathhouse confirmed') score += 8 print(' üìÖ 19th century bathhouse confirmed!') if 'blue minaret' in analysis_text or 'blue-tiled minaret' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Blue-tiled minaret found') score += 12 print(' üïå Blue-tiled minaret found!') if 'shebeke' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Shebeke windows reference found') score += 15 print(' ü™ü Shebeke windows found!') if '5000' in analysis_text or '5,000' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed') score += 12 print(' üé® 5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed!') if 'mirrored balconies' in analysis_text or 'mirror balcon' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Mirrored balconies found') score += 12 print(' ü™û Mirrored balconies found!') if 'wall paintings' in analysis_text or 'wall painting' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Wall paintings reference found') score += 10 print(' üé® Wall paintings found!') if 'eight years' in analysis_text or '8 years' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Eight years construction time found') score += 10 print(' ‚è∞ Eight years construction time found!') if 'traditional houses' in analysis_text and ('verandas' in analysis_text or 'veranda' in analysis_text): found_indicators.append('Traditional houses with verandas found') score += 10 print(' üè† Traditional houses with verandas found!') if 'stained glass' in analysis_text: found_indicators.append('Stained glass windows found') score += 8 print(' üåà Stained glass windows found!') # Store findings if relevant if score >= 8 or len(found_indicators) > 0: finding = { 'search_number': search_idx, 'result_number': result_idx, 'query': query, 'title': title_text, 'body': body_text[:250], # Truncate for storage 'url': url_text, 'score': score, 'indicators': found_indicators } search_findings.append(finding) research_data['findings'].append(finding) print(f' üìã STORED: Score {score}, Indicators: {", ".join(found_indicators)}') print(f' Title: {title_text[:70]}...') # Store search summary search_summary = { 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results), 'findings_count': len(search_findings) } research_data['search_results'].append(search_summary) print(f'\nüìä Search Summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant findings: {len(search_findings)}/{len(results)}') if search_findings: all_search_indicators = [] for finding in search_findings: all_search_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) search_indicator_counts = Counter(all_search_indicators) top_search_indicators = [f"{ind}({count})" for ind, count in search_indicator_counts.most_common(3)] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top indicators: {", ".join(top_search_indicators)}') else: print('‚ùå No results found') research_data['search_results'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': 0, 'findings_count': 0 }) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}') research_data['search_results'].append({ 'query': query, 'error': str(e) }) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n' + '=' * 70) print('PHASE 2: EVIDENCE ANALYSIS') print('=' * 70) total_searches = len(research_data['search_results']) successful_searches = len([s for s in research_data['search_results'] if 'error' not in s]) total_findings = len(research_data['findings']) print(f'Search execution:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {total_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') if research_data['findings']: # Compile all indicators all_indicators = [] for finding in research_data['findings']: all_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) # Analyze evidence frequency indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators) print('\nüìà ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 45) for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions') # Analyze architectural features evidence_analysis = { 'azerbaijan_confirmed': 'Azerbaijan confirmed' in all_indicators, 'sheki_location': 'Sheki location identified' in all_indicators, 'bathhouse_19th_century': ('Bathhouse reference found' in all_indicators and '19th century bathhouse confirmed' in all_indicators), 'blue_tiled_minaret': 'Blue-tiled minaret found' in all_indicators, 'shebeke_5000_pieces': ('Shebeke windows reference found' all_indicators, 'eight_years_construction': 'Eight years construction time found' in all_indicators, 'traditional_houses_verandas': 'Traditional houses with verandas found' in all_indicators, 'stained_glass_windows': 'Stained glass windows found' in all_indicators } research_data['evidence'] = evidence_analysis print('\nüîç ARCHITECTURAL FEATURE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 45) for feature, confirmed in evidence_analysis.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå' print(f'{status} {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}') # Calculate success rate confirmed_count = sum(evidence_analysis.values()) success_rate = (confirmed_count / len(evidence_analysis)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_rate:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(evidence_analysis)} features confirmed)') research_data['success_rate'] = success_rate # Sort findings by score research_data['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP HIGH-SCORE FINDINGS:') print('-' * 40) for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['findings'][:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score: {finding["score"]} | Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])}') print(f' Title: {finding["title"][:90]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Content: {finding["body"][:100]}...') # Analyze locations location_counts = {} for finding in research_data['findings']: content_text = (finding['title'] + ' ' + finding['body']).lower() locations = ['sheki', 'ganja', 'baku', 'gabala', 'quba', 'lahij', 'shamakhi'] for location in locations: if location in content_text: location_counts[location] = location_counts.get(location, 0) + 1 if location_counts: research_data['locations'] = location_counts print('\nüó∫Ô∏è LOCATION ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 25) sorted_locations = sorted(location_counts.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) for location, count in sorted_locations: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {location.title()}: {count} mentions') if sorted_locations: primary_location = sorted_locations[0] research_data['primary_location'] = primary_location[0] print(f'\nüéØ PRIMARY LOCATION: {primary_location[0].title()} ({primary_location[1]} mentions)') else: print('‚ùå No findings collected') # Save results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_architecture_clean_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Create summary report summary = f'''AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE RESEARCH CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION RESULTS Generated: {research_data["timestamp"]} RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features: ''' for feature in research_data['target_features']: summary += f'‚Ä¢ {feature}\n' summary += f''' SEARCH EXECUTION: ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {len(research_data["search_results"])} ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len([s for s in research_data["search_results"] if "error" not in s])} ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {len(research_data["findings"])} ''' if research_data.get('success_rate'): summary += f'‚Ä¢ Research success rate: {research_data["success_rate"]:.1f}%\n' if research_data.get('primary_location'): summary += f'‚Ä¢ Primary location candidate: {research_data["primary_location"].title()}\n' summary += f'''\nARCHITECTURAL FEATURES ANALYSIS:\n''' if research_data.get('evidence'): for feature, confirmed in research_data['evidence'].items(): status = 'CONFIRMED' if confirmed else 'NOT FOUND' summary += f'‚Ä¢ {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {status}\n' summary += f'''\nTOP FINDINGS:\n''' for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['findings'][:3], 1): summary += f'''{i}. {finding["title"]} URL: {finding["url"]} Score: {finding["score"]} Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])} Content: {finding["body"][:120]}... ''' summary += '''FILES GENERATED: ‚Ä¢ azerbaijan_architecture_clean_results.json - Complete research data ‚Ä¢ azerbaijan_architecture_clean_summary.txt - This summary report ''' # Save summary summary_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_architecture_clean_summary.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(summary) print(f'üìã SUMMARY SAVED TO: {summary_file}') print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE RESEARCH COMPLETE - CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION') print('=' * 80) if research_data.get('success_rate', 0) >= 60: print('‚úÖ RESEARCH HIGHLY SUCCESSFUL - Multiple architectural features identified') elif research_data.get('success_rate', 0) >= 40: print('‚ö†Ô∏è RESEARCH MODERATELY SUCCESSFUL - Several features found') else: print('‚ùå LIMITED SUCCESS - Further targeted research recommended') print('\nüìä FINAL STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search queries executed: {len(research_data["search_results"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len([s for s in research_data["search_results"] if "error" not in s])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {len(research_data["findings"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Unique indicators: {len(set(all_indicators)) if research_data["findings"] else 0}') if research_data.get('primary_location'): print(f'\nüéØ PRIMARY LOCATION: {research_data["primary_location"].title()}') if research_data.get('evidence'): confirmed_features = [feature.replace('_', ' ').title() for feature, confirmed in research_data['evidence'].items() if confirmed] if confirmed_features: print('\nüèõÔ∏è CONFIRMED ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for feature in confirmed_features: print(f' ‚úÖ {feature}') print('\n=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE CLEAN RESEARCH COMPLETE ===')

backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') search_findings = [] for result_idx, result in enumerate(results, 1): # len(found_indicators) > 0: finding = { 'search_number': search_idx, 'result_number': result_idx, 'query': query, 'title': title_text, 'body': body_text[:250], # Truncate for storage 'url': url_text, 'score': score, 'indicators': found_indicators } search_findings.append(finding) research_data['findings'].append(finding) print(f' üìã STORED: Score {score}, Indicators: {", ".join(found_indicators)}') print(f' Title: {title_text[:70]}...') # Store search summary search_summary = { 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results), 'findings_count': len(search_findings) } research_data['search_results'].append(search_summary) print(f'\nüìä Search Summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant findings: {len(search_findings)}/{len(results)}') if search_findings: [f"{ind}({count})" for ind, count in search_indicator_counts.most_common(3)] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top indicators: {", ".join(top_search_indicators)}') else: print('‚ùå No results found') successful_searches = len([s for s in research_data['search_results'] if 'error' not in s]) total_findings = len(research_data['findings']) print(f'Search execution:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {total_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {total_findings}') if research_data['findings']: # Compile all indicators all_indicators = [] for finding in research_data['findings']: all_indicators.extend(finding['indicators']) # Analyze evidence frequency indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators) print('\nüìà ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 45) for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions') # Analyze architectural features evidence_analysis = { 'stained_glass_windows': 'Stained glass windows found' in all_indicators } research_data['evidence'] = evidence_analysis print('\nüîç ARCHITECTURAL FEATURE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 45) for feature, confirmed in evidence_analysis.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå' print(f'{status} {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}') # Calculate success rate confirmed_count = sum(evidence_analysis.values()) success_rate = (confirmed_count / len(evidence_analysis)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_rate:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(evidence_analysis)} features confirmed)') research_data['success_rate'] = success_rate # Sort findings by score research_data['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP HIGH-SCORE FINDINGS:') print('-' * 40) for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['findings'][:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score: {finding["score"]} | Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])}') print(f' Title: {finding["title"][:90]}...') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Content: {finding["body"][:100]}...') # Analyze locations location_counts = {} for finding in research_data['findings']: content_text = (finding['title'] + ' ' + finding['body']).lower() locations = ['sheki', 'ganja', 'baku', 'gabala', 'quba', 'lahij', 'shamakhi'] for location in locations: if location in content_text: location_counts[location] = location_counts.get(location, 0) + 1 if location_counts: research_data['locations'] = location_counts print('\nüó∫Ô∏è LOCATION ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 25) sorted_locations = sorted(location_counts.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) for location, count in sorted_locations: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {location.title()}: {count} mentions') if sorted_locations: primary_location = sorted_locations[0] research_data['primary_location'] = primary_location[0] print(f'\nüéØ PRIMARY LOCATION: {primary_location[0].title()} ({primary_location[1]} mentions)') else: print('‚ùå No findings collected') # Save results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_architecture_clean_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Create summary report summary = f'''AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC ARCHITECTURE RESEARCH CLEAN IMPLEMENTATION RESULTS Generated: {research_data["timestamp"]} RESEARCH OBJECTIVE: Identify Azerbaijan historic area with specific architectural features: ''' for feature in research_data['target_features']: summary += f'‚Ä¢ {feature}\n' summary += f''' SEARCH EXECUTION: ‚Ä¢ Total searches: {len(research_data["search_results"])} ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len([s for s in research_data["search_results"] if "error" not in s])} ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {len(research_data["findings"])} ''' if research_data.get('success_rate'): summary += f'‚Ä¢ Research success rate: {research_data["success_rate"]:.1f}%\n' if research_data.get('primary_location'): summary += f'‚Ä¢ Primary location candidate: {research_data["primary_location"].title()}\n' summary += f'''\nARCHITECTURAL FEATURES ANALYSIS:\n''' if research_data.get('evidence'): for feature, confirmed in research_data['evidence'].items(): status = 'CONFIRMED' if confirmed else 'NOT FOUND' summary += f'‚Ä¢ {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {status}\n' summary += f'''\nTOP FINDINGS:\n''' for i, finding in enumerate(research_data['findings'][:3], 1): summary += f'''{i}. {finding["title"]} URL: {finding["url"]} Score: {finding["score"]} Features: {", ".join(finding["indicators"])} Content: {finding["body"][:120]}... ### Development Step 1: Identify China's 1997 Economic Crisis Triggering 287 Billion Yuan Infrastructure Investment

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the significant economic event that China faced in 1997, specifically focusing on the context surrounding China's allocation of 287 billion yuan for major construction projects during that year. Search for keywords including 'China 1997 economic crisis', 'Asian Financial Crisis 1997 China', 'China 287 billion yuan construction projects 1997', '1997 China economic stimulus', and 'China infrastructure investment 1997'. Focus on identifying the specific economic event or crisis that prompted this substantial government investment in construction and infrastructure projects.

**Use Cases**:
- Automated archival research on China‚Äôs 1997 stimulus: a policy historian uses the script to aggregate and score web documents about the 287 billion yuan construction package for a detailed crisis timeline
- Financial due diligence for infrastructure funds: an analyst leverages multi‚Äêengine searches and relevance scoring to verify historical Chinese stimulus measures before structuring new investment products
- Academic literature review on Asian Financial Crisis responses: a university researcher extracts and filters key indicators from global search results to support a peer‚Äêreviewed paper on East Asian policy interventions
- Government planning and risk assessment: a ministry economist integrates search outputs into a dashboard to compare past infrastructure investments during economic shocks for future stimulus planning
- Fact-checking in investigative journalism: a media outlet‚Äôs research team runs the pipeline to validate dates, amounts, and context of China‚Äôs 1997 spending claims across multiple sources
- Macroeconomic risk modeling for fintech: a quant team feeds the cleaned JSON search results into their models to correlate crisis keywords and capital allocations for stress‚Äêtesting portfolios
- Knowledge-graph population for AI assistants: a data engineer imports the structured search data into a corporate knowledge base to enable contextual queries about China‚Äôs 1997 stimulus measures

```
)
```

### Development Step 20: Find Tahir Yuldashev‚Äôs co-founded Islamic organization and the 1992 crackdown perpetrators

- Political risk assessment for an international security consultancy, automatically extracting extremist leaders‚Äô organizational affiliations and crackdown timelines from archived search result JSON files

```
})
```

### Development Step 2: Identify 1997 Chinese Economic Crisis Prompting 287 Billion Yuan Infrastructure Spending

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the significant economic event that China faced in 1997, specifically focusing on the context surrounding China's allocation of 287 billion yuan for major construction projects during that year. Search for keywords including 'China 1997 economic crisis', 'Asian Financial Crisis 1997 China', 'China 287 billion yuan construction projects 1997', '1997 China economic stimulus', and 'China infrastructure investment 1997'. Focus on identifying the specific economic event or crisis that prompted this substantial government investment in construction and infrastructure projects.

**Use Cases**:
- Historical economic research for an academic paper analyzing China‚Äôs infrastructure spending response to the 1997 Asian Financial Crisis
- Government policy evaluation by a fiscal oversight office assessing past stimulus effectiveness through automated search result analysis
- Risk management in a multinational corporation using historical crisis data to inform China market entry strategies
- Financial journalism investigation into China‚Äôs 287 billion yuan investment, extracting key findings for a news feature
- Economic consulting firm automating web‚Äêsearch analysis to benchmark China‚Äôs crisis interventions against other Asian economies
- University business school case study development on sovereign stimulus measures, leveraging structured search result summaries
- Data engineering pipeline integration to ingest search result JSON, filter for relevant economic events, and feed a BI dashboard
- Think-tank policy briefing preparation using synthesized insights on China‚Äôs 1997 stimulus to recommend future infrastructure programs

```
# First, let's inspect the search results file to understand its structure
import json
import os

# Check if the search results file exists and inspect its structure
results_file = 'workspace/china_1997_economic_event_search_results.json'

print("Inspecting the search results file structure...")

if os.path.exists(results_file):
print(f"‚úÖ File found: {results_file}")

# Load and inspect the JSON structure
with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
data = json.load(f)

print(f"\nüìã TOP-LEVEL KEYS:")
for key in data.keys():

print(f" ‚Ä¢ Total queries: {data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}")
print(f" ‚Ä¢ Total results: {data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}")

# Inspect the structure of individual results

print(f"\nüîç SAMPLE RESULT STRUCTURE:")

print(f" ‚Ä¢ {key}: {type(value)} - {str(value)[:100]}{'...' if len(str(value)) > 100 else ''}")

print(f"=" * 70)

high_relevance_results = []
asian_crisis_results = []
infrastructure_results = []

for result in data['all_results']:
title_lower = result.get('title', '').lower()
body_lower = result.get('body', '').lower()
combined_text = f"{title_lower} {body_lower}"

# Check for Asian Financial Crisis mentions
if ('asian financial crisis' in combined_text or 'asian crisis' in combined_text) and '1997' in combined_text:
asian_crisis_results.append(result)

# Check for infrastructure/stimulus mentions with 1997
if ('infrastructure' in combined_text or 'stimulus' in combined_text or 'construction' in combined_text) and '1997' in combined_text:
infrastructure_results.append(result)

# Check for high relevance (multiple key indicators)
relevance_score = result.get('relevance_score', 0)
if relevance_score >= 3:
high_relevance_results.append(result)

print(f"üìà ASIAN FINANCIAL CRISIS 1997 RESULTS: {len(asian_crisis_results)}")
for i, result in enumerate(asian_crisis_results[:5], 1): # Show top 5
print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Key content: {result.get('body', 'No description')[:200]}...")
print(f" Query: {result.get('query_text', 'N/A')}")
print("-" * 50)

print(f"\nüèóÔ∏è INFRASTRUCTURE/STIMULUS 1997 RESULTS: {len(infrastructure_results)}")
for i, result in enumerate(infrastructure_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Key content: {result.get('body', 'No description')[:200]}...")
print("-" * 50)

# Look for the most relevant result that explains the connection
print(f"\n\nüîç MOST RELEVANT FINDING:")
print(f"=" * 40)

# Find results that mention both crisis and China's response
best_results = []
for result in data['all_results']:
combined_text = f"{result.get('title', '').lower()} {result.get('body', '').lower()}"

# Score based on key terms
score = 0
if '1997' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'asian financial crisis' in combined_text: score += 3
if 'china' in combined_text: score += 1
if 'stimulus' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'infrastructure' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'construction' in combined_text: score += 1
if 'investment' in combined_text: score += 1

if score >= 5: # High threshold for best results
best_results.append((score, result))

# Sort by score and show best results
best_results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)

print(f"üèÜ TOP SCORING RESULTS (Score ‚â• 5):")
for i, (score, result) in enumerate(best_results[:3], 1):
print(f"\n{i}. SCORE: {score}")
print(f" Title: {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Description: {result.get('body', 'No description')}")
print(f" Query: {result.get('query_text', 'N/A')}")
print("-" * 60)

# Compile final analysis
print(f"\n\nüìã COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY:")
print(f"=" * 50)
print(f"Total search results analyzed: {len(data['all_results'])}")
print(f"Asian Financial Crisis 1997 mentions: {len(asian_crisis_results)}")
print(f"Infrastructure/stimulus 1997 mentions: {len(infrastructure_results)}")
print(f"High-scoring comprehensive results: {len(best_results)}")

# Save analysis summary

'analysis_timestamp': '2024-12-19',
'economic_event_identified': 'Asian Financial Crisis 1997',

'description': result.get('body', '')[:300]
} for score, result in best_results[:5]]
}

analysis_file = 'workspace/china_1997_economic_event_analysis.json'
with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(analysis_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print("The search results file from the previous step is not available.")
```

from ddgs import DDGS import json import os from datetime import datetime from collections import Counter import time # Targeted search for Sheki Khan's Palace construction timeline and completion date print('=== SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE RESEARCH ===') print('Goal: Identify building that took 8 years for decorative embellishment') print('Focus: Construction dates, completion timeline, decorative work duration') print('=' * 80) # Define targeted search queries for Sheki Khan's Palace construction details search_queries = [ 'Sheki Khan Palace construction date completion Azerbaijan', 'Sheki Khan Palace eight years decorative work embellishment', 'Sheki Palace building timeline construction history', 'Khan Palace Sheki construction years completed when', 'Sheki Khan Palace decorative work duration timeline', 'Azerbaijan Sheki Palace construction 8 years decoration', 'Sheki Khan Palace blue minaret construction date', 'Sheki Palace Shebeke windows construction timeline', 'Khan Palace Sheki historical construction records', 'Sheki Azerbaijan palace building completion date' ] print(f'Starting targeted search with {len(search_queries)} construction-focused queries...') print('Collecting detailed construction timeline information') print('=' * 80) # Initialize search and storage searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) all_search_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Execute searches for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Perform search with multiple backend options results = searcher.text( query, max_results=12, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # Process and display results for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('href', 'No link') snippet = result.get('body', 'No snippet') print(f'\nResult {j}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Link: {link}') print(f'Snippet: {snippet[:250]}...') # Analyze content for construction timeline indicators combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Check for construction timeline indicators timeline_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'khan palace', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'eight years', '8 years', 'decorative', 'embellishment', 'timeline', 'date', 'century', 'minaret', 'shebeke', 'azerbaijan', 'historical', 'architecture' ] matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in timeline_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) if relevance_score >= 4: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') # Store result with analysis all_search_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'sheki_palace_mention': 'sheki' in combined_text and ('khan palace' in combined_text or 'palace' in combined_text), 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'decorative_work_mention': 'decorative' in combined_text or 'embellishment' in combined_text, 'construction_mention': 'construction' in combined_text or 'built' in combined_text or 'completed' in combined_text, 'architectural_features_mention': 'minaret' in combined_text or 'shebeke' in combined_text }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue # Small delay between searches time.sleep(1) print('\n' + '=' * 80) # Create workspace directory if needed if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') #
